[30;1m62 | [0m[35m### Constructor[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35mFor a more granular way of connecting to an SSH server, use the[0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35m`fs.sshfs.SSHFS` constructor, which signature is:[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m67 | [0m[35m```python[0m
[30;1m68 | [0m[35mfrom fs.sshfs import SSHFS[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m40[0m[34m of [0m[33m341[0m[31m ]--[0m

   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m51 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m52 | [0m[35m```python[0m
[30;1m53 | [0m[35mimport fs[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35mmy_fs = fs.open_fs("ssh://[user[:password]@]host[:port]/[directory]")[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35m```[0m
[30;1m56 | [0m[35m[0m
